Within a day a detailed list of what was needed was sent to me along with pics. I think it took five days for us to finally decide to go ahead with most of the recommended the repairs.  Fox Auto team took care of it and finished it ahead of schedule.  We've been taking our cars to Fox for years and trust them to repair our cars right.
Thanks Fox Auto.<//Text>

1) They suggested to replace rotors, a caliper, and pads for $900. When I started asking questions I realized that only front pads need to be replaced. My caliper is in a perfect shape and requires a slight lubrication. My rotors are in a perfect shape as well (VW suggests to replace them at 19mm, but I'm having 21.8 mm now). How did I know that? I doublechecked the brakes myself.

2) According to the maintenance spech, I supposed to change a timing belt and a water pump, but that could be done at a 100,000 miles. Anyway, even VW dillership agreed to change for this labour way cheaper.

<Review>Where do I begin? I go to subway at least 3 times a week. Inside been to many locations from Glendora all the way to Torrance and beyond. This little spot not only makes my sandwiches with a smile but they really take the time here to make your sandwich so that u love eating it.

The place is clean , never dirty and the counters are always sparking.

I have seen some locations that the rugs have lettuce and paper on them because they have not been swept and  because the employees are too lazy or not concerned with the image of the franchise.

This Glendora location is also the closest to me. Distance is not why I'm giving them a 5 star. It's simply their service and friendly vibe and the food never disappoints.

I have had some "So So" sandwiches in locations where the employees look like they don't care and don't like their job.

Randy specifically knows how our sandwiches are made to the exact order of the veggies and dressing order. It does make a difference when you add the vinegar and oil at a specific time and order.

So with all that said , I love this place. I could have had subway in Fontana today but I chose to wait until we arrived in Glendora to eat at the same franchise but at the better location.

You guys rock here in Glendora. Thank for always making us feel like subway is a home made sandwich when we come here!!<//Review><gmapID>0x80c32635d6d6d85b:0x5a3f443e24f21cd2</gmapID>< user_name>

<Name>Christina Fuentes< /Name><time>1618812086992<//time><rate>5< /rate>< Text>
I'm not going to lie in the past I have bounced around nail shops based on the service level & cost. This shop does a great job on eyebrow waxing and I like to get my pedicure done here as well. The prices are reasonable and I have called around to other nail shops that I have gone to before & this shop seems like the only place that has not raised their prices due to Covid which is very much appreciated. The shop has always been very clean & they are honoring social distancing & doing temperatures. Masks are required & there is also a barrier between yourself & the employee. They have lots & lots of nail polish choices too. They accept cash & debit / credit cards however if you do use a card there is an extra charge of either .50 cents or 1.00 sorry I don't remember the exact amount. They are a great shop that I have gone to for well over a decade and I plan on continuing to do so. Thank you Luxury Nails & Spa.</Text>

This would be done by DISINFECTING AND STERILIZATION OF THEIR NAIL EQUIPMENT after each use on a client by placing the equipment in a disinfecting solution or autoclave to prevent contamination from one client to the next.

It would seem that from what I personally witnessed and EXPERIENCE is that Luxury Nails & Spa has decided and clearly choosen not to follow this procedure.

< Review>
I miss the institution in Oakland. I hate having to come all the way to Napa to experience a true Italian delicatessen. But every time I'm in Napa, this is a must-stop place. The clam chowder is extremely delicious with big pieces of clam. They're friendly and move very quickly to get through the long lines. It is worth the wait. My go-to sandwich is the Italian combo with hot coppa added on an onion roll. Other things of note that I've never leave without are the deviled eggs and the stuffed peppers with prosciutto and feta cheese.<//Review>

< Review>
Great Deli!
Depending on the time of day, parking usually very good. Awesome, and high quality sandwich meats. They also serve hot food for lunch specials. High quality desserts. It's a little expensive, but it's worth the price for good quality food.

When you go in, you need to take a ticket with a number on it. With this in mind, they will call out your number when you're up. This is when you place your order. They also have all types of cold salads, macaroni, ravioli, several types of potato salads.

They also offer imported dry foods, which you can't get at other stores. This is a high end Delicatication. They also offer hot soups. I really do appreciate these types eateriess.<//Review>

Well, they have meats, chicken, some salad, etc. When I stated that polenta is usually gf, the man went and asked his co worker and was dismissed as nothing is gf here.
